<rating>5<//rating>< text>
This is mostly in response to the review by Artem:

"Much sugar in there." Yes, they are donuts. Donuts are comprised of sugar. Show me a donut without sugar and I'll show you something that's not a donut.

"No pastries." Yup, once again, you're at a donut shop - not a bakery. If I wanted a pastry, I'd go to a bakery, not a donut shop. Don't give negative critiques to a business that doesn't claim to offer what you're looking for - a low-sugar donut (even though you're apparently looking for pastries).

Johnny's is the best. I live in Concord but thankfully work in Lafayette because Johnny's is the only place I've found that makes donuts worth eating. If you want a real DONUT (not pastry), you'd be smart to check out Johnny's.<//text>

First time here! Mom n Pop owned. I ordered the beef and chicken combo with rice, tomatoes, green pepper, onion, salad, lemon, and bread slices. I was very pleasantly surprised. It smelled so delicious it was mouth watering. And the beef and chicken were slow cooked and moist and tender. The combination of the extras made the meal deliciously filling and satisfying. A great tasty yummy nom noms! I highly recommend to check the place out. Its tiny and cozy. And parking WILL be challenging. But other than that, I was pleasantly surprised at the quality. And of course I washed all this down with my own bottle of reeds extra ginger beer. Delicious. Tasty. Filling. Mouth watering. Nom nom!</Text>

<Review>My Barber's name is David. He goes by "Thy Art" for some reason; I'm guessing his Sensei gave him that name when he was just a young lad in training--or not.

If you're new, he doesn't talk much, and that's okay because he'll give your hair all the attention in the world to get you looking your best.

Once you become a regular, he says a few things like, "what's up? Or "You're late," something of the like.

Also, don't let David's tattoos scare you-- those aren't homie tattoos, they're all done up professionally, so it's meant to be admired.

He's so "hardcore," he says it like it is-- and I appreciate that, even if it hurts. lol

All jokes aside, I've been going to him for a long time now. He's never called out or canceled on me, and has been a reliable friend and barber.

I recommend him for sure, and recommend  the rest of the gang as well. These guys are all veterans in the barber world. You're in great hands.</Review>< GmapID>

< Review>
Innoworld is such a beautiful space to work. I stopped by for a day pass to check out their newest location at Sunnyvale and had the most pleasant and productive experience. The space primarily consists of large private offices, tons of different spaces, super clean bathrooms, kitchen areas and is very hospitable with their free coffee and snacks. Plus, SUPER FAST INTERNET!!

I was impressed by all the light throughout the space. And I cannot forget the awesome staff at the reception desk who gave me a wonderful tour and set me up in a private office for the day to get my work done. I even met some of the members who use the monthly memberships and have their own private offices here. After spending some time in their meeting room and event space, I found this place to fulfill every kind of need, while giving great access to networking opportunities. Amazing experience and a super productive/collaborative work environment. There is always parking room too.

I highly recommend this co-working space if you're looking for a coworking space to work in San Francisco Bay Area.<//Review>

I have completely lost trust in AT&T. I split off from my father‚Äôs plan over 2 years ago (he has been with AT&T since the Cingular days, with 10+ lines for his business.) I went into the corporate store location at 1112 N La Brea Ave in West Hollywood last week to add a line to my account. It was very simple - I was told that my plan would have to be changed from a single line unlimited plan to a multi-line unlimited plan. I was worried about changing the plan, so I asked repeatedly for the rep to confirm that no functionality of my phone would change, and that I would have the same unlimited plan. I was promised that everything would be the same, I would just have the additional line access fee for the new line.

I was traveling for business a few days later and needed to tether to my phone from my laptop to send a few emails. I could not find the hotspot settings in my phone! Assuming this was an error, I called AT&T. I was told that the new plan did not include a hotspot. I couldn‚Äôt believe this, as it was reiterated again and again that I was not ‚Äúdowngrading‚Äù my plan. I literally couldn‚Äôt believe that this was truly the case, so I texted the rep who I worked with (he gave me his card and circled his cell number on it) and he blatantly lied to me and told me that ‚Äúwe went over the hotspot options‚Äù and I agreed to downgrade my plan. This is a typical bait-and-switch tactic and SUPER shady. I absolutely did not expect this from AT&T. I‚Äôm not here to waste time - if we had that conversation, why would I be so surprised that I no longer have hotspot access?

So now my only option is to pay an additional $25/mo plus tax in order to upgrade my plan to the ‚Äúpremium‚Äù option, which includes hotspot through my phone. That would bring my total monthly cost to about $150/mo, while I can get 4 lines of unlimited with hotspot access through t-mobile for $120/mo! I‚Äôm really not happy about this. I will be returning the new phone and canceling my entire plan. I hate knowing that a company my family has trusted (and paid!) for almost 20 years is so willing to be dishonest and rip me off.< /Review>
